 ;CODE MEMORY: (0x00000000-0x0000FFFF) 
 ;DATA MEMORY: (0x00010000-0x0001FFFF) 

 org 0000 

 mfc0 $16, $13
 beq $16, $0, _reset

 exception_handler: 
	mfc0 $16, $12
	mfc0 $17, $13
	mfc0 $19, $14
	mfc0 $20, $15
	sw $16, 0($29)
	sw $17, 4($29)
	sw $19, 8($29)
	sw $20, 12($29)
	addi $19, $19, 4
	mtc0 $19, $14
	mfc0 $21, $12
	addi $21, $21, 65533
	ori $21, $21, 1
	mtc0 $21, $12
	cop0 4
	jr $19

 _reset: 
	xor $0, $0, $0
	xor $1, $1, $1
	xor $2, $2, $2
	xor $3, $3, $3
	xor $4, $4, $4
	xor $5, $5, $5
	xor $6, $6, $6
	xor $7, $7, $7
	xor $8, $8, $8
	xor $9, $9, $9
	xor $10, $10, $10
	xor $11, $11, $11
	xor $12, $12, $12
	xor $13, $13, $13
	xor $14, $14, $14
	xor $15, $15, $15
	xor $16, $16, $16
	xor $17, $17, $17
	xor $18, $18, $18
	xor $19, $19, $19
	xor $20, $20, $20
	xor $21, $21, $21
	xor $22, $22, $22
	xor $23, $23, $23
	xor $24, $24, $24
	xor $25, $25, $25
	xor $26, $26, $26
	xor $27, $27, $27
	xor $28, $28, $28
	xor $29, $29, $29
	xor $30, $30, $30
	xor $31, $31, $31

 main:
;........other test........;
;........reset $26 back for branch loops........;
 lui $26, 0
;........reset $28 back for other test loops........;
 lui $28, 0
;........set memory location for signature........;
 lui $29, 1
 ori $29, $29, 6000

 jal reset_offsets
 jal init_cp
 j syscalls

syscalls:
	syscall

;..........data-path test..........;
 lui $29, 1
 ori $29, $29, 10000

jal reset_offsets
jal init_cp

	lw $15, 0($30)
	lw $16, 4($30)
	jr $31

	lui $30, 1
	ori $30, $30, 8
	xor $27, $27, $27
	xor $18, $18, $18
	jr $31
